<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:montage.html>montage</a> (18580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:montage.html>montage</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mount.html>mount</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mont</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mount.html>mount</a>(ain)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mons</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mountain.html>mountain</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-age</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mooier.html>mooier</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mooist.html>mooist</a></b>)

***moonrise.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moonrise.html>moonrise</a> (60016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:moon.html>moon</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rise.html>rise</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:moonrise.html>moonrise</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">moonrises</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:time.html>time</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:day.html>day</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:night.html>night</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:when.html>when</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moon.html>moon</a> begins <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rise.html>rise</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horizon.html>horizon</a>.
<ul><li><b>1742</b>, Matthew <a href = vnd.unilang:towers.html>Towers</a> (translator), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lyric.html>Lyric</a> Pieces <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horace" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Horace">Horace</a></i>, Dublin, <a href = vnd.unilang:volume.html>Volume</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>I</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ode.html>Ode</a> III, <a href = vnd.unilang:p.html>p</a>. 17,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://catalog.hathitrust.org/Record/009779780">[1]</a></sup>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:moral.html>moral</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mōrālis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">relating <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> manners <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morals.html>morals</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:morbide.html>morbide</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">morbidus</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>morbid
